# M10 Units #1–7, #15 — ḥāṭāʾ sin-act family (shared-substrate family file)

- **File:** wa-m10-units-01to07-15-hatat-sinact-family-v1-20260623.md · **v1 · 2026-06-23 · Author:** Claude Code.
- **Units (source: sin-core):** #1 Wilful sinning · #2 Unintentional sinning · #3 Confession · #4 Conscience suppression · #5 Refusal to repent · #6 Habitual defection · #7 Contagious sin · #15 Generational sin. (These are the **act-mode** units of the sin verb — the ways the act of sinning is committed, owned, denied, repeated, transmitted, inherited.)
- **Substrate:** cha.ta (H2398, Hebrew sin-verb "to sin") + hamartanō (G0264, NT sin-verb "to sin") + paraptōma (G3900, "trespass/transgression"). 263 occ / 263 verses in the per-verse section.
- **What this file is:** the self-contained evidence home for the eight act-mode units — **(A)** general observations on the whole sin-act field + flags, then the eight unit sub-sections (collated from the source digests HA / HM / R2p — *nothing of note left behind*), and **(B)** the per-verse structured substrate (once; shared across the units; the generator emits full lexical for every term). Flag markers per the index method. Evidence only; **highlight, do not resolve.**
- **Index:** `wa-m10-unit-index-1to32-v1-20260623.md`. **Scope note:** the source digests **HA (ḥāṭāʾ family)** and **HM (hamart- family)** are **partially migrated** here — specifically these units' **act-modes** (the verb cha.ta H2398, the verb hamartanō G0264, and paraptōma G3900). The ḥāṭāʾ **NOUNS** (chat.tat H2403B / chet H2399 / cha.ta.ah H2401 / chat.ta H2400 "sinner") and the hamart- nouns carry the *status/record/forgiveness/sinner-type* faces and belong to units **#11–#14 / #16** (still pending) — they are **not** fully migrated by this file. HA/HM remain provenance for those.

---

## A. General observations (whole sin-act field)

**Mechanical signature — cha.ta (H2398, HA digest §1).** The verb reads `action` (211 of 213 occ = the act of sinning) with **faculty `moral_evaluation`** as a **term-intrinsic** property of the head verb (NOT a verse-level reading). Top senses: sinned 79 / sin 51 / committed 19. Valence overwhelmingly `sinful`; object_type frequently `(none)` or `abstract` (the sin is defined by the breached commandment, not a governed object). Book spread: the verb sits in the legal (Lev/Num), prophetic (Eze/Isa/Jer), penitential (Psa) and narrative (Gen/1Ki/2Ki/1Sa) corpus.

**Mechanical signature — hamartanō (G0264) within the hamart- family (HM digest §1).** The whole hamart- family carries **faculty `volition` on ALL 191 occ** — a sharp **cross-language contrast** with the faculty-none Hebrew core terms (see ⚑ SYNTH below). The verb hamartanō (37 occ) reads `action`; valence `sinful` 183 / `forbidden` 5 (the "sin no more / do not sin" imperatives) / `neutral` 3 (the marriage/self-humbling cases where the act is denied). Rom dominant in the family (48), then Luk/Joh/Mat/Mar.

**Mechanical signature — paraptōma (G3900, R2p digest §1).** "Trespass" — Pauline, type-status, tightly **paired with grace and forgiveness** ("dead in trespasses" Eph 2:1,5; "not counting their trespasses" 2Cor 5:19; Adam's trespass Rom 5). Minimal intrinsic inner-being content — a juridical/relational status with the remedy sitting right beside it.

- **⚠ HYGIENE — the chat.tat DOUBLE SENSE (sin AND sin offering).** The single most important diversity in the ḥāṭāʾ group: the same lemma names both the offense (chat.tat H2403B = "sin", 160 occ, all status/sinful) **and** its cultic remedy (chat.tat H2403H = "sin offering", 110 occ, sense "sin offering", valence neutral 57 / commanded 31 / (none) 7 / sinful 14 / righteous 1). Any consumer that collapses H2403B + H2403H would mis-read the offering occ as sinful. Keep the sub-entries distinct. **Note: the sin-offering belongs to unit #14 (Forgiveness), NOT to the act-mode units in this file** — flagged here only because it shares the lemma. The verb cha.ta H2398 (this file's substrate) is the *act*, not the offering. Num 15:27 carries BOTH in one verse (cha.ta "to sin" + chat.tat "sin offering"). **Surface, not resolved.**
- **The cha.ta registers (HA §2b — three settings of the one verb, held open).** (b1) Levitical legal "if anyone sins **unintentionally**" frame (→ #2); (b2) prophetic/penitential register, Psa 51 / 2Sa 24:10 / 1Ki 8:47 / Exo 32:30 "you have sinned a great sin" (→ #1/#3); (b3) relational "sinned against God/you" register, object_type=God on 55 occ, Gen 39:9 / Psa 41:4 / Gen 20:6 / 1Sa 19:5 (→ #1). The verb carries all three with one form — **held open whether one phenomenon in three settings or distinct faces.**
- **Bounded heart-seating (HA §2e — the genuine inner signal, sparse).** Of 38 co-seated cha.ta occ the genuine **heart**-seatings are ≈15 of 547 across the group — the interior is **bounded, not pervasive**. Genuine heart (lev/le.vav) seats on the SIN VERB: Exo 9:34 (Pharaoh "sinned yet again and **hardened his heart**"); 2Sa 24:10 ("David's **heart** struck him… I have sinned"); 1Ki 8:47 ("if they turn their **heart**… 'We have sinned'"); Jer 17:1 (sin "engraved on the tablet of their **heart**"); Gen 20:6 ("integrity of your **heart**… kept you from sinning"); Lev 19:17 ("not hate your brother in your **heart**… lest you incur sin"); Deu 15:9 ("unworthy thought in your **heart**… you be guilty of sin"); 2Ki 10:31 ("not careful to walk… with all his **heart**… did not turn from the sins"); Job 1:5 ("my children… cursed God in their **hearts**"); Psa 4:4 ("do not sin; ponder in your own **hearts**"). flesh (ba.sar, 3): Num 16:22; Psa 38:3; Hos 8:13. **⚠ HYGIENE — the ne.phesh idiom (over-read caution):** of the 20 co-seated ne.phesh occ MOST are the "life/soul" idiom ("hunt my life", "poured out his soul to death", "sin against innocent blood/life"), NOT soul-seating; AND the Levitical "if anyone (nephesh) sins" frame uses nephesh as the grammatical subject "person/anyone". Do not read nephesh-as-person as soul-seating. Genuine resonance only: Eze 18:20 ("the **soul** who sins shall die"); Mic 6:7; Hos 4:8. The NT seats (HM §2f) are a different, richer web — pneuma/sarx/nous/psuchē/kardia/suneidesis, Romans-concentrated — but those attach to the noun hamartia (dominion register, → #12), not to the act-verb units here. **⚠ HYGIENE — faculty is term-intrinsic** on both cha.ta (`moral_evaluation`) and the whole hamart- family (`volition`); verse-level inner engagement must read from co-terms/co-seated, never from the faculty tag. **⚠ HYGIENE — object vs object_type:** trust object_type (e.g. Exo 9:34 object="heart" but object_type=abstract; Exo 32:30 object="sin" type=abstract). object=(none) on 284 is correct silence on status-noun usages, not a gap.
- **⚑ SYNTH — the atonement seam.** The chat.tat sin-offering sense + Lev 16:30 cleansing + Psa 51:2 "cleanse me from my sin" are the *remedy* face built into the sin-word — part of the atonement mechanism alongside the sin-offering and kip.pu.rim (see units #14 + the exploration threads). The removing-side of sin belongs with the dealing-with-sin apparatus, not the act-mode units. **Surface for the atonement synthesis.**
- **⚑ SYNTH — the faculty=volition cross-language seam (the §10 test case).** The NT hamart- family is uniformly tagged `volition` while the Hebrew sin-terms read faculty-none. Held open: is this a real linguistic fact (the Greek sin-words genuinely encode an act-of-the-will — sin as a *characteristic of the will*) or a uniform tagging convention masking the same status/verdict character? Bears directly on whether sin is ontologically a *status* or a *faculty-engaged characteristic*. This matters acutely for #1 (Wilful sinning = the will committing a known wrong). **Surface, not resolved.**
- **⚖ BORDER — status / action / quality split.** Across the ḥāṭāʾ group the verb reads `action`, the status-nouns `status`, the person-noun chat.ta `quality` — held open whether this is a real ontological distinction or a **POS artefact**. The act-mode units in this file are the `action` face; the `status`/`quality` faces belong to #11–#14/#16.

**↔ BOND (cross-cluster, for §A — these act-mode units bond dominantly with):**
- **↔ BOND — M26 (Righteousness)** — the structural antithesis; sinner-vs-righteous, "turns from righteousness and does injustice" (Eze 18/33), the sin↔righteousness pole-pair that frames the whole act-field.
- **↔ BOND — M11 (Repentance / Forgiveness)** — the turning-from / being-forgiven counterpart; afiēmi the standing partner of hamartanō (the paralytic forgiveness cluster); shuv "turn" the partner of cha.ta; especially #3 (Confession) and #5 (Refusal to repent).
- **↔ BOND — M12 (Purity)** — cleanse/purify the remedy register (Lev 16:30; Psa 51:2); the atonement-seam bond.
- **↔ BOND — M47 (Constitution / seats)** — the heart/flesh/mind/spirit seats that sin engages (lev/le.vav/ba.sar; pneuma/sarx/nous/kardia/suneidesis); the bounded-interior evidence above feeds any M47 cross-reference.
- **↔ BOND — M38 (Salvation)** — "to save sinners" (1Ti 1:15), the borne-for / died-for-our-sins register (Joh 1:29; 1Cor 15:3) that answers the sin-act.
- **↔ BOND — M41 (Remembrance)** *for #5 specifically* — refusal to repent links to remembrance/forgetting of the LORD (the covenant-memory axis; the "did not turn" register pairs with remembering/forgetting God).

**⚖ BORDER — shared-substrate / per-occurrence assignment (governing for this file).** Units #2 (Unintentional), #7 (Contagious), and #15 (Generational) are **all carried by the same verb cha.ta** and are distinguished **only by reading**, not by lemma. Likewise #1 vs #3 vs #4 vs #5 vs #6 all draw on cha.ta / hamartanō. Salient verses are assigned below **only where the reading is CLEAR** (the named registers — Lev "if anyone sins unintentionally" for #2; "I have sinned" confessions for #3; "made Israel to sin" for #7; "visiting iniquity of the fathers" for #15). **Per-occurrence assignment beyond the clear cases is DEFERRED to §10.** Overlap across units is expected and washes out in analysis.

---

### Unit #1 — Wilful sinning
- **DEF (DB):** The will committing a known wrong; a deliberate relational act — the person knows and does it.
- **Observations (HA §2b2, §2b3; HM §2c).** The deliberate "you have sinned a great sin" register: Exo 32:30 ("You have sinned a great sin"). The relational "sinned against God / you" register (object_type=God, 55 occ): Gen 39:9 ("how then can I do this great wickedness and sin against God"); Psa 41:4 ("I have sinned against you"); 1Sa 19:5 ("sin against innocent blood"). NT deliberate sinning: Heb 10:26 ("if we go on **sinning deliberately** after receiving the knowledge of the truth"); the brother who "sins against you" (Mat 18:15,21; Luk 17:3,4). The faculty=volition tag on the whole hamart- family (HM §1) bears directly here.
- **Salient (clear reading):** Exo 32:30; Gen 39:9; Psa 41:4; 1Sa 19:5; Heb 10:26.
- **⚑ SYNTH:** the faculty=volition seam (see §A) is the live question for "wilful" — is the will-engagement a real lexical fact or a family tag? **Surface.**

### Unit #2 — Unintentional sinning
- **DEF (DB):** Sin without deliberate intent; conscience engages once it surfaces (the Levitical "if anyone sins unintentionally" frame — Lev 4–5; Num 15).
- **Observations (HA §2b1 — PRIMARY home).** The Levitical legal frame: "If anyone sins **unintentionally** in any of the Lord's commandments" (Lev 4:2,22,27; 5:15; Num 15:24,27,28); "and realizes his guilt" (Lev 4:27) — conscience engaging on awareness. Object_type frequently (none)/abstract; the sin is defined by the breached commandment, not a governed object. **⚠ HYGIENE:** the "if anyone (nephesh) sins" subject is nephesh-as-person, NOT soul-seating (assembly correctly does not tag these co-seated).
- **Salient (clear reading):** Lev 4:2; Lev 4:22; Lev 4:27; Lev 5:15; Num 15:24; Num 15:27; Num 15:28.
- **⚖ BORDER:** shares the cha.ta verb with #7/#15 — distinguished only by the "unintentionally" reading. Beyond the named Lev/Num frame, assignment deferred to §10.

### Unit #3 — Confession
- **DEF (DB):** The inner person names a committed sin as sin (Psa 51; 2Sa 24:10 "I have sinned"; 1Ki 8:47).
- **Observations (HA §2b2; HM §2c).** The penitential/confessional register: Psa 51:2,4,5 ("Against you, you only, have I sinned… in sin did my mother conceive me"); 2Sa 24:10 ("I have sinned greatly in what I have done"); 1Ki 8:47 ("We have sinned and have acted perversely"). NT first-person confession: Mat 27:4 ("I have sinned by betraying innocent blood"); Luk 15:18,21 (the prodigal: "Father, I have sinned against heaven and before you"). Heart-seated: 2Sa 24:10 (David's **heart** struck him); 1Ki 8:47 ("turn their **heart**").
- **Salient (clear reading):** Psa 51:4; 2Sa 24:10; 1Ki 8:47; Mat 27:4; Luk 15:18; Luk 15:21.
- **⚖ BORDER — #3 vs #4 (opposite conscience-responses, shared terms):** Confession (#3, the inner person NAMES the sin) and Conscience suppression (#4, the inner person DENIES/suppresses awareness) are the **opposite conscience-responses to the same cha.ta verb**, distinguished only by reading. Salient assignment beyond the clear "I have sinned" cases deferred to §10.

### Unit #4 — Conscience suppression
- **DEF (DB):** Does not recognize / denies / suppresses awareness of own sin (the OPPOSITE of #3).
- **Observations (HA §2b1, §2e; HM §2c).** Lev 5:1 ("If anyone sins in that he hears a public adjuration… yet **does not speak**, he shall bear his iniquity") — suppressed disclosure. The hardened-heart register: Exo 9:34 (Pharaoh "**sinned yet again and hardened his heart**") — the heart-seated refusal to recognise. Joh 9:41 ("If you were blind, you would have no **guilt**; but now that you say, 'We see,' your guilt remains") — denial of one's own sin keeps it. 1Jo 1:10 ("If we say we have not sinned, we make him a liar") — denial of having sinned at all.
- **Salient (clear reading):** Lev 5:1; Exo 9:34; Joh 9:41; 1Jo 1:10.
- **⚖ BORDER:** the opposite of #3 (see #3); same cha.ta substrate, distinguished by the suppress/deny reading.

### Unit #5 — Refusal to repent
- **DEF (DB):** The will persistently refuses to turn when departure is available / required.
- **Observations (HA §2e; HM §2c).** The "did not turn from the sins" register: 2Ki 10:31 ("Jehu was **not careful to walk** in the law of the Lord… with all his **heart**; he **did not turn** from the sins of Jeroboam"). The persisting-in-sin NT seam: Heb 10:26 (going on sinning deliberately after the knowledge of the truth); 1Jo 3:6,8,9 (the one who "keeps on sinning"); Joh 8:21,24 ("you will **die in your sin**" — refusal that ends unrepented). Persistent refusal pairs with shuv "turn" (M11).
- **Salient (clear reading):** 2Ki 10:31; Heb 10:26; Joh 8:21; Joh 8:24.
- **↔ BOND:** #5 also bonds **M41 (Remembrance)** — the refusal to turn tracks forgetting / not remembering the LORD (the covenant-memory axis), in addition to the dominant M11 (Repentance).

### Unit #6 — Habitual defection
- **DEF (DB):** Sin as a recurring established pattern over time.
- **Observations (HA §2c; HM §2c).** The persisting "sins of Jeroboam" line in 1Ki/2Ki (a settled recurring pattern transmitted and repeated — overlaps #7). The sinner-type as a standing person who habitually sins (HA §2c, chat.ta H2400 — but that NOUN is #16; the act-pattern here is the verb). NT habitual-sinning set (1 John): 1Jo 3:6 ("No one who abides in him keeps on sinning"); 1Jo 3:8,9; 1Jo 5:16,18; Joh 8:34 ("everyone who **practices** sin is a slave to sin" — the practising/habitual frame). Exo 9:34 "sinned **yet again**" = repetition.
- **Salient (clear reading):** Joh 8:34; 1Jo 3:6; 1Jo 3:8; 1Jo 3:9; Exo 9:34.
- **⚖ BORDER:** the recurring-pattern reading overlaps #7 (Jeroboam line is both habitual and contagious) — assignment of shared "sins of Jeroboam" verses deferred to §10.

### Unit #7 — Contagious sin
- **DEF (DB):** Sin set by a leader and transmitted to those under authority (Jeroboam "made Israel to sin" register).
- **Observations (HA §4 mapping).** The causative "made Israel to sin" register — a leader's sin transmitted to those under his authority (the recurring 1Ki/2Ki refrain attached to Jeroboam: "the sins of Jeroboam… which he **made Israel to sin**", e.g. 2Ki 10:31). Num 16:22 carries the corporate-contagion question explicitly: "O God, the God of the spirits of all flesh, **shall one man sin, and will you be angry with all the congregation?**" — sin's spread from one to the body.
- **Salient (clear reading):** Num 16:22; 2Ki 10:31 (the "made Israel to sin" refrain; the causative Hiphil of cha.ta is the marker).
- **⚖ BORDER:** #2/#7/#15 share the identical verb cha.ta, distinguished only by reading (unintentional vs leader-transmitted vs lineage-inherited). The causative ("made… to sin") is the #7 marker; salient assignment of the full Jeroboam-refrain set deferred to §10.

### Unit #15 — Generational sin
- **DEF (DB):** Sin inherited through lineage (the "visiting iniquity of the fathers" register).
- **Observations (HA §4 mapping).** The lineage register: Num 32:14 ("And behold, you have risen in your fathers' place, **a brood of sinful men**, to increase still more the fierce anger of the Lord against Israel") — sin propagated down the generations. The persisting "sins of Jeroboam" line as inherited (overlaps #6/#7). The classic "visiting the iniquity of the fathers on the children" register is the named frame for this unit (carried in the a.von/iniquity material, AV digest — cross-referenced; the cha.ta substrate here gives Num 32:14 directly). **⚠ HYGIENE:** the "visiting iniquity of fathers" verses are primarily a.von-noun (AV digest), not cha.ta — the cha.ta substrate contributes Num 32:14; the full lineage register draws on AV (per the index, #15 = DB · HA · AV).
- **Salient (clear reading):** Num 32:14 (the cha.ta substrate's clear lineage verse).
- **⚖ BORDER:** shares cha.ta with #2/#7; the lineage/inheritance reading is the #15 marker. The fuller "iniquity of the fathers" corpus sits in AV (not this substrate) — flagged so synthesis pulls AV for #15.

---

## B. Per-verse structured evidence (shared substrate, once)
> Generated from the corpus (`_build_m10_unit_verse_evidence_20260623.py --strongs H2398,G0264,G3900`). The eight units above draw their salient verses from this substrate; the generator emits **full lexical for every term** (self-standing). Per-occurrence axis-assignment (which verse → which unit) is **deferred to §10** except where flagged salient above. **⚖ BORDER:** units #1–#7 and #15 share the cha.ta / hamartanō / paraptōma substrate — verse→unit assignment is by reading, not lemma.

_Per-verse structured evidence — 263 verses; Strong's ['G0264', 'G3900', 'H2398']. From the corpus; evidence only._
